< Text>
This is a nice big park. I come here with some folks to play cricket. There is a small play area as well where families can bbq as well. Nice big parking lot. There is a also a big baseball field there. Cricket pitch is based on first come first serve basis. Basically it is a hard ball practice pitch area. I have seen folks come with their dogs and play. Some folks bring their drones and RC helicopters to play there.</Text>

< review>
This is a popular, well kept park. There is plenty of grass and fenced in fields for either baseball or for dogs to run around in off leash. There's also a basketball court and a paved loop for a quick walk.  Young kids also have a playground they can explore.  I normally visit the park during lunch and there are always people enjoying the park.< /review>

< text>
Uhm, what?! Did NOT expect this to taste THIS good! I'm usually skeptical when it comes to Asian-fusion burgers, but this place somehow got it down right. Their kalbi burger marinade is just perfect (not too sweet) and their patty meat feels very high quality and lean. You don't get the greasy, miserable feeling after eating. And whatever they did to add the crispy outer layer‚ÄîYUM! Adds such a beautiful texture. Look at how neatly they wrap everything too, so it's easy to hold your burger without getting your hands messy. It's the little things! Sweet potato fries were also amazing, gives Chick Fil A waffle fries a run for their money.<//text>

Amazing food and amazing staff/service!  Ordered two chicken burgers, normal fries, and sweet potato fries. My partner has a shellfish allergy and the chef was very accommodating and offered to fry his food in the fryer that was not used for the crab burger to lower risk of cross contamination. <user_id>113055638209640464714</user_id><name>Ash Valentine</name><Time>1564816875681< /Time>< Rate>
3</Rate>
< text>
~Service
The cashier was very friendly and properly took my order down. Food took within 15 minutes, but didn't mind because I knew that the meal was being cooked the second I ordered it.

~Food
Chicken Burger plus avocado and bacon with fries were $15.88. Chicken burger had a great, flavorful presentation. The bacon, crispy chicken, lettuce, and other ingredients brought the burger to life but that's not how I felt when I bit into it. The BBQ sauce that was on it was displeasing, I didn't like the taste of the chicken, very messy burger to eat, and it didn't give me any passion when eating the burger. I advise to leave the 2 sheets of paper on the burger so it doesn't slip and slide out your hands. Maybe this choice of burger just wasn't for me. The fries on the other hand were nice. They gave me In & Out vibes because they lacked heavily seasoned salt and tasted more baked than fried. I enjoy the ketchup, it tasted healthier, like tomato paste and I enjoyed that with the fries. I also liked the on-side pickles that was served with the meal.

~Overall
Even though I didn't like the chicken burger with an addition of avocado and bacon very much, doesn't mean I didn't enjoy the crispy, light fries and the very friendly and welcoming environment!</text>

< Text>
Very friendly staff. Food is incredible! The chicken sammich has a good crispness to it and is not dry at all. The presentation and construction of the sammich is organized and not messy.

The funnel cake fries are super tasty and sweet enough as is so you don't have to dip in syrup.

Funnel cake is delicious.

Panko breaded tenders were juicy and goes great with their sauces. Garlic cheese sauce is addicting! The curry mayo was a nice change of taste when eating the tenders.

The sweet potato fries are really good. I usually hate them when I go to lazy dog or many or restaurants. It's cripsy and not mushy at all. Has a balance of tasting enough like fries but with s sweet potato hint.

I would highly suggest everyone eat here. I finished the whole meal of everything above. I don't usually eat that much but it was so good I could not stop. Even now I want to order and eat more! Go here!< /Text>

<UserId.>106642025232199339027<//UserId.><Name>Ron G<//Name><date>1556352299023<//date><Rate>5<//Rate>< review>
We stumbled upon it and got attracted  by the simple design of the restaurant.  We were received with open arms by the chef/owner.  He advised we try the Portobello burger and we did. We also tried the sunnyburst breakfast sandwich.  The were both amazing.  The Portobello tasted like a light slice of fried beef and brought out a special taste that I have never taste in a Portobello.  The Sunnyburst sandwich had egg and bacon with a bit of pineapple dressing that helped bring the full flavor of the sandwich.  The Snozzberry was a huge surprise, I couldn't describe the taste of it but could not stop drinking it.  To me it tasted like how a candy or drink from Willy Wonka would taste if it existed.  Amazing.  The fish and chips tasted good too.  The fish was light and delicious. The chips further brought out the flavor of the fish.  The chocolate balls were to die for.  They tasted like carnival funnel cake but better because it had an actual hazel nut and it was amazing.  The cheese balls was delicious too.  Even though they were made of cheese, the outer part was made from the same layer of funnel cake but it tasted better especially with the maple syrup that they provided.  The customer service was amazing and we will be returning to try other menu items in the near future.  I highly recommend Crispy School for others to try.</review>

What happened:
I bought a Subaru Legacy 2013 with a little over 150,000 miles on it. I was given Carfax information and negotiated a price of $6,400 (not including taxes and fees). I test drove the car and found no problem except I did think I felt a wobble of the car when I braked, but my father (who was with me) and I felt it may have just been the road.
I wanted to buy the car right away, but I couldn't get everything involving my car loan taken care of in time, so I let Shoman Motors know that I wanted to purchase it two days later (the day after Thanksgiving).
They said okay and I went 2 days later to purchase the car. I had negotiated $6,400 and they had me pay an extra $153 in fees (not taxes or registration since I was taking the car to another state to register it).
By this point I had talked to all 3 owners/partners: one father and two sons. I paid the $153 and filled out the paperwork my bank and the dealership gave me. Shoman Motors had no working fax machine so they asked me to email the dealer funding request to my bank.
Next I took my new car home, about 30 miles away. Two days later, as I was driving on the freeway the wobble returned. It happened twice -one minute apart- and I immediately stopped the car and took it to the closest auto repair shop open. After a $143 diagnostic, they told me the lower front left and right arm controls were bad and needed to be replaced immediately. I called Shoman Motors and told them the issue. By now I had driven the car about 80 miles total since buying it. They answered my calls (and called me back) and ended up telling me that I could either return the car entirely to them for a $150 fee, or I could take my car to them and they would order and replace the 2 controller arms at the cost of the parts and wave the mechanic fees. They told me they sold me the car at a low market price for the value and so they wouldn't be able to reimburse me for the diagnostic fee nor would the pay to buy the parts needed and replace them for free. So I decided to bring they car back to Shoman Motors to have them repair the car. Went I arrived to turn in my car they told me it would be about or around $300. I said okay and gave them my keys. They were able to get the needed parts the next morning and had the car repaired by 12:30pm. When I went back in to pay the cost of the parts they said it was $300 even. My father was with me and asked for an itemized report. They told us that it was at their other office and they wouldn't be able to give it to me because their printer was broken. However they could email it to me later. We mentioned the price for the parts for the car should not have been that high. We were told $300 was the price I agreed on. They then charged the card for $500 instead of $300. I noticed the error and the card was refunded $200. I then took my keys and left.

My opinion:
All 3 owners were kind. However, if you are going to have your own business: have a working printer and fax machine. Get a pair of scissors for all of your offices so you are not handing your customers ripped paper. Know what your other partners are saying to your customers. Tell your customers about warranty opportunities. And never, ever, overcharge someone.</review>

For the past four and a half years, Los Tapatios (and the former name escapes me) has set the standard for me in San Diego's "Mexican Cuisine Scene" as one of my top three favorite joints period. Their California Burrito is especially delicious, but their plates and combos are also some of the best I've had in the city. My only complaint is the reduction in options from their salsa bar, but I can understand that from a business perspective so it's all good.< /review>

< Review>
The upside to the Wooden Horse is that one can pick out almost any toy in stock and it will be a good, quality toy. Being a "store", one can expect to pay more for a given toy than buying it on-line or elsewhere but the time savings and the benefit of buying "local" have, in the past, outweighed cost savings. Recently however I bought a Lego gift and noticed afterwards the added cost of buying it at the Wooden Horse was much higher than it was in the past. I paid a 30% premium for buying the product at the Wooden Horse vs at the Lego Store. This has crossed a line for me. Their return policy is credit or exchange only so can't get a refund but I won't make the same mistake again.< /Review>

There is also a trail to walk on the backside of the water and a big picnic area with bbqs and tables with plenty of room for a big get together. Really nice Vietnamese restaurant in Lawndale. Monday night for dinner wasn‚Äôt too busy so got a table right away. Their stir fried filet mignon with onions was great, not overcooked and can be ordered low carb style. It came with this beef broth bowl that was so good, super clean with the right amount of savory. Also got the bun cha pork combo with egg rolls, shrimp, and noodles which gives you a nice taste of a few things. Finally finished with Vietnamese spring rolls, which were nicely layered, and the combo pho with beef slices, tripe, tendon etc. Only thing I would change is the pho meat was just slightly over cooked. And get the Vietnamese coffee on the way out when you pay at the counter, one of the best things I got. Not too sweet, but full of coffee flavor.< /text>

<date>1604166777487</date><Name>Cody Remy< /Name>< text>
We came here on a Friday night and it was relatively busy. Service was terribly slow and the wait staff had to be waved down for anything, even though they appeared to spend a lot of time meandering around between serving plates. The staff appears very inexperienced and their method of clearing tables and serving food was very inefficient. The server also made a small error in our order and charged us for a larger soup.

The filet mignon pho was excellent, and the broth had a lot of flavor. My guest on the other hand said the seafood pho was "okay" and was clearly made with frozen seafood that did not taste fresh. We ordered an appetizer of egg rolls which were disgusting. They were mushy and still partly frozen in the middle, and the outside shell was flaking and falling apart. I was surprised to discover a place like this was serving frozen rolls.

Overall, some of the soup was really good, but overall the food and service was disappointing. There are plenty of other options in Gardena.<//text>

<name>David Kelley<//name><Time>1518326689378< /Time><Rating>5</Rating><review>Place usually packed, wait time 20-40 minutes.  They accept evening reservations of 5 or more people, any less and you wait in line.
Decent selection of noodle soups, my wife prefers the rare beef, I always choose seafood. Prices about $7 for the small, up to $12.75 for the extra large.  If you order the extra large, spring for extra noodles too! Pepper, hoisin sauce and Thai hot sauce on all the tables. There is a generous offering of traditional Vietnamese dishes, the combo fried rice with various meats looks really good. The only drawback to this marvelous little spot is the payment process. They will bring your bill to the table, but they will not take your payment at the table. Instead you form a line to the cash register to pay your bill. The line is long and slow, my wife spent nearly as much time waiting in line to pay our bill as she spent eating her incredibly delicious pho selection. I recommend a update their payment process.< /review>< pics>
